29 void Boxologic::encode()
30 {
31  // READ_BOXLIST_INPUT
32  pallet.width = wrapper->getContainableWidth();
33  pallet.height = wrapper->getContainableHeight();
34  pallet.length = wrapper->getContainableLength();
35 
36  box_array.assign(instanceArray->size() + 1, struct BoxInfo());
37  layer_map.clear();
38  total_boxes = instanceArray->size();
39 
40  for (size_t i = 0; i < instanceArray->size(); i++)
41  {
42  shared_ptr<Instance> instance = instanceArray->at(i);
43  size_t k = i + 1;
44 
45  box_array[k].width = instance->getWidth();
46  box_array[k].height = instance->getHeight();
47  box_array[k].length = instance->getLength();
48 
49  box_array[k].volume = instance->getVolume();
50  box_array[k].is_packed = false;
51  }
52 
53  // INITIALIZE
54  temp = 1.0;
55  pallet.volume = temp * pallet.width * pallet.height * pallet.length;
56  total_box_volume = 0.0;
57 
58  for (size_t x = 1; x <= total_boxes; x++)
59  total_box_volume = total_box_volume + box_array[x].volume;
60 
61  scrap_list.emplace_back();
62 
63  best_solution_volume = 0.0;
64  packing_best = false;
65  hundred_percent = false;
66  number_of_iterations = 0;
67 }
68 
69 void Boxologic::decode()
70 {
71  wrapper->clear();
72  leftInstanceArray->clear();
73 
74  for (size_t k = 1; k <= total_boxes; k++)
75  {
76  const BoxInfo &box = box_array[k];
77  shared_ptr<Instance> instance = instanceArray->at(k - 1);
78 
79  if (box.is_packed == true)
80  {
81  Wrap *wrap = new Wrap(wrapper.get(), instance,box.cox, box.coy, box.coz);
82  wrap->estimateOrientation(box.layout_width, box.layout_height, box.layout_length);
83 
84  wrap->setPosition
85  (
86  wrap->getX() + wrapper->getThickness(),
87  wrap->getY() + wrapper->getThickness(),
88  wrap->getZ() + wrapper->getThickness()
89  );
90  wrapper->emplace_back(wrap);
91  }
92  else
93  {
94  // 공간 부족으로 포장에 실패한 잔여 물체의 경우 leftInstanceArray->push_back(instance); } } // 정렬 sort(wrapper->begin(), wrapper->end(), [](const shared_ptr<Wrap> &left, const shared_ptr<Wrap> &right) -> bool { if (left->getZ() != right->getZ()) return left->getZ() < right->getZ(); else if (left->getY() != right->getY()) return left->getY() < right->getY(); else return left->getX() < right->getX(); }); } /* ----------------------------------------------------------- GETTERS ----------------------------------------------------------- */ auto Boxologic::fetch_scrap_min_z_left() -> list<struct Scrappad>::iterator { if (scrap_min_z == scrap_list.begin()) return scrap_list.end(); else { auto it = scrap_min_z; it--; return it; } } auto Boxologic::fetch_scrap_min_z_right()->list<struct Scrappad>::iterator { auto it = scrap_min_z; it++; return it; } /* ----------------------------------------------------------- OPERATORS ----------------------------------------------------------- */ auto Boxologic::pack() -> pair<shared_ptr<Wrapper>, shared_ptr<InstanceArray>> { execute_iterations(); report_results(); decode(); return {wrapper, leftInstanceArray}; } void Boxologic::execute_iterations(void) { for (variant = 1; variant <= 6; variant++) { switch (variant) { case 1: pallet.layout_width = pallet.width; pallet.layout_height = pallet.height; pallet.layout_length = pallet.length; break; case 2: pallet.layout_width = pallet.length; pallet.layout_height = pallet.height; pallet.layout_length = pallet.width; break; case 3: pallet.layout_width = pallet.length; pallet.layout_height = pallet.width; pallet.layout_length = pallet.height; break; case 4: pallet.layout_width = pallet.height; pallet.layout_height = pallet.width; pallet.layout_length = pallet.length; break; case 5: pallet.layout_width = pallet.width; pallet.layout_height = pallet.length; pallet.layout_length = pallet.height; break; case 6: pallet.layout_width = pallet.height; pallet.layout_height = pallet.length; pallet.layout_length = pallet.width; break; } list_candidate_layers(); for (auto it = layer_map.begin(); it != layer_map.end(); it++) { ++number_of_iterations; packed_volume = 0.0; packedy = 0; packing = true; layer_thickness = it->first; itelayer = it->first; remainpy = pallet.layout_height; remainpz = pallet.layout_length; packed_boxes = 0; for (size_t x = 1; x <= total_boxes; x++) { // 모든 박스를 다시 빼냄 box_array[x].is_packed = false; } //BEGIN DO-WHILE do { layerinlayer = 0; layerdone = 0; if (pack_layer()) { exit(1); } packedy = packedy + layer_thickness; remainpy = pallet.layout_height - packedy; if (layerinlayer) { prepackedy = packedy; preremainpy = remainpy; remainpy = layer_thickness - prelayer; packedy = packedy - layer_thickness + prelayer; remainpz = lilz; layer_thickness = layerinlayer; layerdone = 0; if (pack_layer()) { exit(1); } packedy = prepackedy; remainpy = preremainpy; remainpz = pallet.layout_length; } find_layer(remainpy); } while (packing); // END DO-WHILE if (packed_volume > best_solution_volume) { // 최적 packing 정보를 갱신 // 이 정보들은 따로이 구조화가 필요하다 best_solution_volume = packed_volume; best_variant = variant; best_iteration = itelayer; number_packed_boxes = packed_boxes; } // 공간을 100% 다 활용했다면 끝냄 if (hundred_percent) break; pallet_volume_used_percentage = best_solution_volume * 100 / pallet.volume; } // 공간을 100% 다 활용했다면 끝냄 if (hundred_percent) break; // 정육면체라면, orientation은 6으로 고정 if ((pallet.width == pallet.height) && (pallet.height == pallet.length)) variant = 6; } } void Boxologic::list_candidate_layers() { double exdim; // 기준으로 삼을 축에서의 크기 double dimdif; double dimen2, dimen3; // 기준 외 잔여 축에서의 크기 size_t x, y, z; double layereval; for (x = 1; x <= total_boxes; x++) { for (y = 1; y <= 3; y++) { // 기준 축으로부터 기준 크기 (key) 를 뽑아옴 switch (y) { case 1: exdim = box_array[x].width; boxy = dim2; boxz = dim3; bfx = hmx - dim1; bfy = hy - dim2; bfz = abs(hz - dim3); boxi = x; } else if (hy - dim2 == bfy && hmx - dim1 < bfx) { boxx = dim1; boxy = dim2; boxz = dim3; bfx = hmx - dim1; boxi = x; } } else { if (dim2 - hy < bbfy) { bboxx = dim1; bboxy = dim2; bboxz = dim3; bbfx = hmx - dim1; bbfy = dim2 - hy; bbfz = abs(hz - dim3); bboxi = x; } else if (dim2 - hy == bbfy && hmx - dim1 < bbfx) { bboxx = dim1; bboxz = dim3; bbfx = hmx - dim1; bbfy = dim2 - hy; bbfz = abs(hz - dim3); bboxi = x; } } } } void Boxologic::find_smallest_z() { scrap_min_z = scrap_list.begin(); for (auto it = scrap_list.begin(); it != scrap_list.end(); // } // scrapmemb = scrapmemb->next; //} //return; } void Boxologic::checkfound() { evened = 0; if (boxi) { cboxi = boxi; cboxx = boxx; cboxy = boxy; cboxz = boxz; } else { auto &left = fetch_scrap_min_z_left(); } void Boxologic::volume_check() { box_array[cboxi].is_packed = true; box_array[cboxi].layout_width = cboxx; box_array[cboxi].layout_height = cboxy; box_array[cboxi].layout_length = cboxz; packed_volume = packed_volume + box_array[cboxi].volume; hundred_percent = true; } return; } void Boxologic::report_results(void) { switch (best_variant) { case 1: pallet.layout_width = pallet.width; pallet.layout_height = pallet.height; pallet.layout_length = pallet.length; pallet.layout_height = pallet.height; pallet.layout_length = pallet.length; break; case 2: pallet.layout_width = pallet.length; pallet.layout_height = pallet.height; pallet.layout_length = pallet.width; pallet.layout_height = pallet.length; pallet.layout_length = pallet.width; break; } list_candidate_layers(); for (auto it = layer_map.begin(); it != layer_map.end(); it++) { ++number_of_iterations; packed_volume = 0.0; lenz = left->cumz - scrap_min_z->cumz; lpz = remainpz - scrap_min_z->cumz; find_box(lenx, layer_thickness, remainpy, lenz, lpz); checkfound(); if (layerdone) break; if (evened) continue; box_array[cboxi].coy = packedy; // ERASE FROM MIN_Z TO RIGHT auto right_of_right = right; right_of_right++; // RIGHT'S RIGHT OR END MAYBE //scrap_list.erase(scrap_min_z, right_of_right); //scrap_min_z = scrap_list.end(); scrap_min_z = scrap_list.erase(scrap_min_z, right_of_right); // free(scrap_min_z); //} } else { scrap_min_z->cumz += cboxz; } } else if (left->cumx < pallet.layout_width - scrap_min_z->cumx) { if (scrap_min_z->cumz + cboxz == left->cumz) { // WEIRDO PART // BOX_ARRAY[CBOXI].COX IS DOUBLY MINUSED scrap_min_z->cumx -= cboxx; box_array[cboxi].cox = scrap_min_z->cumx; //box_array[cboxi].cox = scrap_min_z->cumx - cboxx; } else { box_array[cboxi].cox = left->cumx; // CREATE A NODE BETWEEN LEFT AND MIN_Z struct Scrappad node = { left->cumx + cboxx, scrap_min_z->cumz + cboxz }; scrap_list.insert(scrap_min_z, node); //// CREATE A NODE BETWEEN LEFT AND MIN_Z //scrap_min_z->prev->next = (struct Scrappad*)malloc(sizeof(struct Scrappad)); //if (scrap_min_z->prev->next == NULL) //{ // cout << "Insufficient memory available" << endl; //(scrap_min_z->prev)->cumz = scrap_min_z->cumz + cboxz; } } else { if (scrap_min_z->cumz + cboxz == left->cumz) { left->cumx += cboxx; box_array[cboxi].cox = left->cumx; } else { box_array[cboxi].cox = scrap_min_z->cumx - cboxx; right = fetch_scrap_min_z_right(); box_array[cboxi].coy = packedy; box_array[cboxi].coz = scrap_min_z->cumz; box_array[cboxi].cox = left->cumx; if (cboxx == scrap_min_z->cumx - left->cumx) { if (scrap_min_z->cumz + cboxz == left->cumz) { // LEFT FETCHES MIN_Z'S left->cumx = scrap_min_z->cumx; //(scrap_min_z->prev)->cumz = scrap_min_z->cumz + cboxz; } } volume_check(); } } return 0; } int Boxologic::find_layer(double thickness) { double exdim, dimdif, dimen2, dimen3; double layereval, eval; z <= total_boxes; z++) { if (!(x == z) && !(box_array[z].is_packed)) { dimdif = abs(exdim - box_array[z].width); if (abs(exdim - box_array[z].height) < dimdif) { dimdif = abs(exdim - box_array[z].height); } if (abs(exdim - box_array[z].length) < dimdif) { dimdif = abs(exdim - box_array[z].length); } layereval = layereval + dimdif; } } if (layereval < eval) { eval = layereval; layer_thickness = exdim; } } } } if (layer_thickness == 0 || layer_thickness > remainpy) packing = false; return 0; } void Boxologic::find_box(double hmx, double hy, double hmy, double hz, double hmz) { bfx = 32767; bfy = 32767; bfz = 32767; bbfx = 32767; bbfy = 32767; bbfz = 32767; boxi = 0; bboxi = 0; for (size_t x = 1; analyze_box(x, hmx, hy, hmy, hz, hmz, box_array[x].height, box_array[x].length, box_array[x].width); analyze_box(x, hmx, hy, hmy, hz, hmz, box_array[x].length, box_array[x].width, box_array[x].height); analyze_box(x, hmx, hy, hmy, hz, hmz, box_array[x].length, box_array[x].height, box_array[x].width); } } void Boxologic::analyze_box(size_t x, double hmx, double hy, double hmy, double hz, double hmz, double dim1, double dim2, double dim3) { if (dim1 <= hmx && dim2 <= hmy && dim3 <= hmz) { if (dim2 <= hy) { if (hy - dim2 < bfy) { boxx = dim1; boxy = dim2; boxz = dim3; bfx = hmx - dim1; bfy = hy - dim2; bfz = abs(hz - dim3); boxi = x; } else if (hy - dim2 == bfy && hmx - dim1 < bfx) { boxx = dim1; boxy = dim2; boxz = dim3; bfx = hmx - dim1; bfy = hy - dim2; bfz = abs(hz - dim3); boxi = x; } else if (hy - dim2 == bfy && hmx - dim1 == bfx && abs(hz - dim3) < bfz) { boxx = dim1; boxy = dim2; boxz = dim3; bfx = hmx - dim1; bfy = hy - dim2; bfz = abs(hz - dim3); boxi = x; } } else { if (dim2 - hy < bbfy) { bboxx = dim1; bboxy = dim2; bboxz = dim3; bbfx = hmx - dim1; bbfy = dim2 - hy; bbfz = abs(hz - dim3); bboxi = x; } else if (dim2 - hy == bbfy && hmx - dim1 < bbfx) { bboxx = dim1; bboxz = dim3; bbfx = hmx - dim1; bbfy = dim2 - hy; bbfz = abs(hz - dim3); bboxi = x; } } } } void Boxologic::find_smallest_z() { scrap_min_z = scrap_list.begin(); for (auto it = scrap_list.begin(); it != scrap_list.end(); // } // scrapmemb = scrapmemb->next; //} //return; } void Boxologic::checkfound() { evened = 0; if (boxi) { cboxi = boxi; cboxx = boxx; cboxy = boxy; cboxz = boxz; } else { auto &left = fetch_scrap_min_z_left(); } void Boxologic::volume_check() { box_array[cboxi].is_packed = true; box_array[cboxi].layout_width = cboxx; box_array[cboxi].layout_height = cboxy; box_array[cboxi].layout_length = cboxz; packed_volume = packed_volume + box_array[cboxi].volume; hundred_percent = true; } return; } void Boxologic::report_results(void) { switch (best_variant) { case 1: pallet.layout_width = pallet.width; pallet.layout_height = pallet.height; pallet.layout_length = pallet.length; break; case 2: pallet.layout_width = pallet.length; pallet.layout_height = pallet.height; pallet.layout_length = pallet.width; break; case 3: pallet.layout_width = pallet.length; pallet.layout_height = pallet.width; pallet.layout_length = pallet.height; break; case 4: pallet.layout_width = pallet.height; pallet.layout_height = pallet.width; pallet.layout_length = pallet.length; break; case 5: pallet.layout_width = pallet.width; pallet.layout_height = pallet.length; pallet.layout_length = pallet.height; break; case 6: pallet.layout_width = pallet.height; pallet.layout_height = pallet.length; pallet.layout_length = pallet.width; break; } packing_best = true; packed_box_percentage = best_solution_volume * 100 / total_box_volume; pallet_volume_used_percentage = best_solution_volume * 100 / pallet.volume; list_candidate_layers(); packed_volume = 0.0; packedy = 0; packing = true; layer_thickness = best_iteration; remainpy = pallet.layout_height; remainpz = pallet.layout_length; for (size_t x = 1; x <= total_boxes; x++) { box_array[x].is_packed = false; } do { layerinlayer = 0; layerdone = 0; pack_layer(); packedy = packedy + layer_thickness; remainpy = pallet.layout_height - packedy; if (layerinlayer) { prepackedy = packedy; preremainpy = remainpy; remainpy = layer_thickness - prelayer; packedy = packedy - layer_thickness + prelayer; remainpz = lilz; layer_thickness = layerinlayer; layerdone = 0; pack_layer(); packedy = prepackedy; remainpy = preremainpy; remainpz = pallet.layout_length; } find_layer(remainpy); } while (packing); } void Boxologic::write_boxlist_file() { double x, y, z, bx, by, bz; switch (best_variant) { case 1: x = box_array[cboxi].cox; y = box_array[cboxi].coy; z = box_array[cboxi].coz; bx = box_array[cboxi].layout_width; by = box_array[cboxi].layout_height; bz = box_array[cboxi].layout_length; break; case 2: x = box_array[cboxi].coz; y = box_array[cboxi].coy; z = box_array[cboxi].cox; bx = box_array[cboxi].layout_length; by = box_array[cboxi].layout_height; bz = box_array[cboxi].layout_width; break; case 3: x = box_array[cboxi].coy; y = box_array[cboxi].coz; z = box_array[cboxi].cox; bx = box_array[cboxi].layout_height; by = box_array[cboxi].layout_length; bz = box_array[cboxi].layout_width; break; case 4: x = box_array[cboxi].coy; y = box_array[cboxi].cox; z = box_array[cboxi].coz; bx = box_array[cboxi].layout_height; by = box_array[cboxi].layout_width; bz = box_array[cboxi].layout_length; break; case 5: x = box_array[cboxi].cox; y = box_array[cboxi].coz; z = box_array[cboxi].coy; bx = box_array[cboxi].layout_width; by = box_array[cboxi].layout_length; bz = box_array[cboxi].layout_height; break; case 6: x = box_array[cboxi].coz; 100  sort(wrapper->begin(), wrapper->end(),
101  [](const shared_ptr<Wrap> &left, const shared_ptr<Wrap> &right) -> bool
102  {
103  if (left->getZ() != right->getZ())
104  return left->getZ() < right->getZ();
105  else if (left->getY() != right->getY())
106  return left->getY() < right->getY();
107  else
108  return left->getX() < right->getX();
109  });
110 }

112 /* -----------------------------------------------------------
113  GETTERS
114 ----------------------------------------------------------- */
115 auto Boxologic::fetch_scrap_min_z_left() -> list<struct Scrappad>::iterator
116 {
117  if (scrap_min_z == scrap_list.begin())
118  return scrap_list.end();
119  else
120  {
121  auto it = scrap_min_z;
122  it--;
123 
124  return it;
125  }
126 }
127 
128 auto Boxologic::fetch_scrap_min_z_right()->list<struct Scrappad>::iterator
129 {
130  auto it = scrap_min_z;
131  it++;
132 
133  return it;
134 }

136 /* -----------------------------------------------------------
137  OPERATORS
138 ----------------------------------------------------------- */
139 auto Boxologic::pack() -> pair<shared_ptr<Wrapper>, shared_ptr<InstanceArray>>
140 {
141  execute_iterations();
142  report_results();
143 
144  decode();
145 
146  return {wrapper, leftInstanceArray};
147 }
148 
149 void Boxologic::execute_iterations(void)
150 {
151  for (variant = 1; variant <= 6; variant++)
152  {
153  switch (variant)
154  {
155  case 1:
156  pallet.layout_width = pallet.width;
157  pallet.layout_height = pallet.height;
158  pallet.layout_length = pallet.length;
159  break;
160  case 2:
161  pallet.layout_width = pallet.length;
162  pallet.layout_height = pallet.height;
163  pallet.layout_length = pallet.width;
164  break;
165  case 3:
166  pallet.layout_width = pallet.length;
167  pallet.layout_height = pallet.width;
168  pallet.layout_length = pallet.height;
169  break;
170  case 4:
171  pallet.layout_width = pallet.height;
172  pallet.layout_height = pallet.width;
173  pallet.layout_length = pallet.length;
174  break;
175  case 5:
176  pallet.layout_width = pallet.width;
177  pallet.layout_height = pallet.length;
178  pallet.layout_length = pallet.height;
179  break;
180  case 6:
181  pallet.layout_width = pallet.height;
182  pallet.layout_height = pallet.length;
183  pallet.layout_length = pallet.width;
184  break;
185  }
186 
187  list_candidate_layers();
188 
189  for (auto it = layer_map.begin(); it != layer_map.end(); it++)
190  {
191  ++number_of_iterations;
192 
193  packed_volume = 0.0;
194  packedy = 0;
195  packing = true;
196 
197  layer_thickness = it->first;
198  itelayer = it->first;
199  remainpy = pallet.layout_height;
200  remainpz = pallet.layout_length;
201  packed_boxes = 0;
202 
203  for (size_t x = 1; x <= total_boxes; x++)
204  {
205  // 모든 박스를 다시 빼냄
206  box_array[x].is_packed = false;
207  }
208 
209  //BEGIN DO-WHILE
210  do
211  {
212  layerinlayer = 0;
213  layerdone = 0;
214 
215  if (pack_layer())
216  {
217  exit(1);
218  }
219  packedy = packedy + layer_thickness;
220  remainpy = pallet.layout_height - packedy;
221 
222  if (layerinlayer)
223  {
224  prepackedy = packedy;
225  preremainpy = remainpy;
226  remainpy = layer_thickness - prelayer;
227  packedy = packedy - layer_thickness + prelayer;
228  remainpz = lilz;
229  layer_thickness = layerinlayer;
230  layerdone = 0;
231 
232  if (pack_layer())
233  {
234  exit(1);
235  }
236 
237  packedy = prepackedy;
238  remainpy = preremainpy;
239  remainpz = pallet.layout_length;
240  }
241  find_layer(remainpy);
242  }
243  while (packing);
244  // END DO-WHILE
245 
246  if (packed_volume > best_solution_volume)
247  {
248  // 최적 packing 정보를 갱신 // 이 정보들은 따로이 구조화가 필요하다 best_solution_volume = packed_volume; best_variant = variant; best_iteration = itelayer; number_packed_boxes = packed_boxes; } // 공간을 100% 다 활용했다면 끝냄 if (hundred_percent) break; pallet_volume_used_percentage = best_solution_volume * 100 / pallet.volume; } // 공간을 100% 다 활용했다면 끝냄 if (hundred_percent) break; // 정육면체라면, orientation은 6으로 고정 if ((pallet.width == pallet.height) && (pallet.height == pallet.length)) variant = 6; } } void Boxologic::list_candidate_layers() { double exdim; // 기준으로 삼을 축에서의 크기 double dimdif; double dimen2, dimen3; // 기준 외 잔여 축에서의 크기 size_t x, y, z; double layereval; for (x = 1; x <= total_boxes; x++) { for (y = 1; y <= 3; y++) { // 기준 축으로부터 기준 크기 (key) 를 뽑아옴 switch (y) { case 1: exdim = box_array[x].width; dimen2 = box_array[x].height; dimen3 = box_array[x].length; break; case 2: exdim = box_array[x].height; dimen2 = box_array[x].width; dimen3 = box_array[x].length; break; case 3: exdim = box_array[x].length; dimen2 = box_array[x].width; dimen3 = box_array[x].height; break; } if ((exdim > pallet.layout_height) || (((dimen2 > pallet.layout_width) || (dimen3 > pallet.layout_length)) && ((dimen3 > pallet.layout_width) || (dimen2 > pallet.layout_length)))) { // 박스가 화물칸보다 큰 경우 continue; } // 기존 레이어와 중복되면 SKIP if (layer_map.count(exdim) != 0) continue; layereval = 0; // 모든 박스의 최소 크기 (각 박스의 x, y, z축 내 최소 크기) 를 구하여 // 현재 레이어에 쌓는다 (layereval에 더한다) for (z = 1; z <= total_boxes; z++) { if (!(x == z)) { dimdif = abs(exdim - box_array[z].width); if (abs(exdim - box_array[z].height) < dimdif) { dimdif = abs(exdim - box_array[z].height); } if (abs(exdim - box_array[z].length) < dimdif) { dimdif = abs(exdim - box_array[z].length); } layereval = layereval + dimdif; } } // 레이어 크기와 기준값을 기록함 layer_map[exdim] = layereval; } } return; } int Boxologic::pack_layer() { double lenx, lenz, lpz; if (!layer_thickness) { packing = false; return 0; } scrap_list.begin()->cumx = pallet.layout_width; /*scrap_min_z->next = (struct Scrappad*)malloc(sizeof(struct Scrappad)); if (scrap_min_z->next == NULL) { printf("Insufficient memory available\n"); return 1; } scrap_min_z->next->next = NULL; scrap_min_z->next->prev = scrap_min_z; //(scrap_min_z->prev)->cumz = scrap_min_z->cumz + cboxz; } } volume_check(); } } return 0; } int Boxologic::find_layer(double thickness) { double exdim, dimdif, dimen2, dimen3; double layereval, eval; layer_thickness = 0; eval = 1000000; size_t y, z; for (size_t x = 1; x <= total_boxes; x++) { if (box_array[x].is_packed) continue; for (y = 1; y <= 3; y++) { switch (y) { case 1: exdim = box_array[x].width; dimen2 = box_array[x].height; dimen3 = box_array[x].length; break; case 2: exdim = box_array[x].height; dimen2 = box_array[x].width; dimen3 = box_array[x].length; break; case 3: exdim = box_array[x].length; dimen2 = box_array[x].width; dimen3 = box_array[x].height; break; } layereval = 0; if ((exdim <= thickness) && (((dimen2 <= pallet.layout_width) && (dimen3 <= pallet.layout_length)) || ((dimen3 <= pallet.layout_width) && (dimen2 <= pallet.layout_length)))) { for (z = 1; z <= total_boxes; z++) { if (!(x == z) && !(box_array[z].is_packed)) { dimdif = abs(exdim - box_array[z].width); if (abs(exdim - box_array[z].height) < dimdif) { dimdif = abs(exdim - box_array[z].height); } if (abs(exdim - box_array[z].length) < dimdif) { dimdif = abs(exdim - box_array[z].length); } layereval = layereval + dimdif; } } if (layereval < eval) { eval = layereval; layer_thickness = exdim; } } } } if (layer_thickness == 0 || layer_thickness > remainpy) packing = false; return 0; } void Boxologic::find_box(double hmx, double hy, double hmy, double hz, double hmz) { bfx = 32767; bfy = 32767; bfz = 32767; bbfx = 32767; bbfy = 32767; bbfz = 32767; boxi = 0; bboxi = 0; for (size_t x = 1; x <= total_boxes; x++) { if (box_array[x].is_packed) continue; if (x > total_boxes) return; analyze_box(x, hmx, hy, hmy, hz, hmz, box_array[x].width, box_array[x].height, box_array[x].length); if ((box_array[x].width == box_array[x].length) && (box_array[x].length == box_array[x].height)) continue; analyze_box(x, hmx, hy, hmy, hz, hmz, box_array[x].width, box_array[x].length, box_array[x].height); analyze_box(x, hmx, hy, hmy, hz, hmz, box_array[x].height, box_array[x].width, box_array[x].length); analyze_box(x, hmx, hy, hmy, hz, hmz, box_array[x].height, box_array[x].length, box_array[x].width); analyze_box(x, hmx, hy, hmy, hz, hmz, box_array[x].length, box_array[x].width, box_array[x].height); analyze_box(x, hmx, hy, hmy, hz, hmz, box_array[x].length, box_array[x].height, box_array[x].width); } } void Boxologic::analyze_box(size_t x, double hmx, double hy, double hmy, double hz, double hmz, double dim1, double dim2, double dim3) { if (dim1 <= hmx && dim2 <= hmy && dim3 <= hmz) { if (dim2 <= hy) { if (hy - dim2 < bfy) { boxx = dim1; boxy = dim2; boxz = dim3; bfx = hmx - dim1; bfy = hy - dim2; bfz = abs(hz - dim3); boxi = x; } else if (hy - dim2 == bfy && hmx - dim1 < bfx) { boxx = dim1; boxy = dim2; boxz = dim3; bfx = hmx - dim1; bfy = hy - dim2; bfz = abs(hz - dim3); boxi = x; } else if (hy - dim2 == bfy && hmx - dim1 == bfx && abs(hz - dim3) < bfz) { boxx = dim1; boxy = dim2; boxz = dim3; bfx = hmx - dim1; bfy = hy - dim2; bfz = abs(hz - dim3); boxi = x; } } else { if (dim2 - hy < bbfy) { bboxx = dim1; bboxy = dim2; bboxz = dim3; bbfx = hmx - dim1; bbfy = dim2 - hy; bbfz = abs(hz - dim3); bboxi = x; } else if (dim2 - hy == bbfy && hmx - dim1 < bbfx) { bboxx = dim1; bboxy = dim2; bboxz = dim3; bbfx = hmx - dim1; bbfy = dim2 - hy; bbfz = abs(hz - dim3); bboxi = x; } else if (dim2 - hy == bbfy && hmx - dim1 == bbfx && abs(hz - dim3) < bbfz) { bboxx = dim1; bboxy = dim2; bboxz = dim3; bbfx = hmx - dim1; bbfy = dim2 - hy; bbfz = abs(hz - dim3); bboxi = x; } } } } void Boxologic::find_smallest_z() { scrap_min_z = scrap_list.begin(); for (auto it = scrap_list.begin(); it != scrap_list.end(); it++) if (it->cumz < scrap_min_z->cumz) scrap_min_z = it; //struct Scrappad *scrapmemb = scrap_first; //scrap_min_z = scrapmemb; //while (!(scrapmemb->next == NULL)) //{ // if (scrapmemb->next->cumz < scrap_min_z->cumz) // { // scrap_min_z = scrapmemb->next; // } // scrapmemb = scrapmemb->next; //} //return; } void Boxologic::checkfound() { evened = 0; if (boxi) { cboxi = boxi; cboxx = boxx; cboxy = boxy; cboxz = boxz; } else { auto &left = fetch_scrap_min_z_left(); auto &right = fetch_scrap_min_z_right(); if ((bboxi > 0) && (layerinlayer || (left == scrap_list.end() && right == scrap_list.end()))) { //////////////////////////////////////////// // ~ OR SCRAP_MIN_Z HAS NO NEIGHBOR //////////////////////////////////////////// if (!layerinlayer) { prelayer = layer_thickness; lilz = scrap_min_z->cumz; } cboxi = bboxi; cboxx = bboxx; cboxy = bboxy; cboxz = bboxz; layerinlayer = layerinlayer + bboxy - layer_thickness; layer_thickness = bboxy; } else { if (left == scrap_list.end() && right == scrap_list.end()) { ////// // ^~ AND SCRAP_MIN_Z HAS NO NEIGHBOR ////// layerdone = true; } else { evened = true; if (left == scrap_list.end()) { /////////////////////////////////////////// // NO LEFT, BUT RIGHT /////////////////////////////////////////// // ERASE SCRAP_MIN_Z // RIGHT IS THE NEW SCRAP_MIN_Z scrap_min_z = scrap_list.erase(scrap_min_z); //struct Scrappad *trash = scrap_min_z->next; //scrap_min_z->cumx = scrap_min_z->next->cumx; //scrap_min_z->cumz = scrap_min_z->next->cumz; //scrap_min_z->next = scrap_min_z->next->next; //if (scrap_min_z->next) //{ // scrap_min_z->next->prev = scrap_min_z; //} //free(trash); } else if (right == scrap_list.end()) { /////////////////////////////////////////// // NO RIGHT, BUT LEFT /////////////////////////////////////////// // ERASE CURRENT SCRAP_MIN_Z // THE LEFT ITEM FETCHES MIN'S CUM_X left->cumx = scrap_min_z->cumx; // ERASE FROM MIN_Z TO END //scrap_list.erase(scrap_min_z, scrap_list.end()); //scrap_min_z = scrap_list.end(); scrap_min_z = scrap_list.erase(scrap_min_z, scrap_list.end()); //scrap_min_z->prev->next = NULL; //scrap_min_z->prev->cumx = scrap_min_z->cumx; //free(scrap_min_z); } else { /////////////////////////////////////////// // LEFT & RIGHT ARE ALL EXIST /////////////////////////////////////////// if (left->cumz == right->cumz) { // ---------------------------------------- // LEFT AND RIGHT'S CUM_Z ARE EQUAL // ---------------------------------------- // LEFT FETCHES THE RIGHT'S CUM_X left->cumx = right->cumx; // ERASE MIN AND ITS RIGHT auto right_of_right = right; right_of_right++; //scrap_list.erase(scrap_min_z, right_of_right); //scrap_min_z = scrap_list.end(); scrap_min_z = scrap_list.erase(scrap_min_z, right_of_right); } void Boxologic::volume_check() { box_array[cboxi].is_packed = true; box_array[cboxi].layout_width = cboxx; box_array[cboxi].layout_height = cboxy; box_array[cboxi].layout_length = cboxz; packed_volume = packed_volume + box_array[cboxi].volume; hundred_percent = true; } return; } void Boxologic::report_results(void) { switch (best_variant) { case 1: pallet.layout_width = pallet.width; pallet.layout_height = pallet.height; pallet.layout_length = pallet.length; pallet.layout_height = pallet.length; pallet.layout_length = pallet.height; break; case 6: pallet.layout_width = pallet.height; pallet.layout_height = pallet.length; pallet.layout_length = pallet.width; break; } packing_best = true; packed_box_percentage = best_solution_volume * 100 / total_box_volume; pallet_volume_used_percentage = best_solution_volume * 100 / pallet.volume; list_candidate_layers(); } do { layerinlayer = 0; layerdone = 0; pack_layer(); packedy = packedy + layer_thickness; remainpy = pallet.layout_height - packedy; if (layerinlayer) { prepackedy = packedy; preremainpy = remainpy; remainpz = pallet.layout_length; } find_layer(remainpy); } while (packing); } void Boxologic::write_boxlist_file() { double x, y, z, bx, by, bz; switch (best_variant) { case 1: x = box_array[cboxi].cox; analyze_box(x, hmx, hy, hmy, hz, hmz, box_array[x].height, box_array[x].length, box_array[x].width); analyze_box(x, hmx, hy, hmy, hz, hmz, box_array[x].length, box_array[x].width, box_array[x].height); analyze_box(x, hmx, hy, hmy, hz, hmz, box_array[x].length, box_array[x].height, box_array[x].width); } } void Boxologic::analyze_box(size_t x, double hmx, double hy, double hmy, double hz, double hmz, double dim1, double dim2, double dim3) { if (dim1 <= hmx && dim2 <= hmy && dim3 <= hmz) { if (dim2 <= hy) { if (hy - dim2 < bfy) { boxx = dim1; boxy = dim2; boxz = dim3; bfx = hmx - dim1; bfy = hy - dim2; bfz = abs(hz - dim3); boxi = x; } else if (hy - dim2 == bfy && hmx - dim1 < bfx) { boxx = dim1; boxy = dim2; boxz = dim3; bfx = hmx - dim1; bfy = hy - dim2; bfz = abs(hz - dim3); boxi = x; } else if (hy - dim2 == bfy && hmx - dim1 == bfx && abs(hz - dim3) < bfz) { boxx = dim1; boxy = dim2; boxz = dim3; bfx = hmx - dim1; bfy = hy - dim2; bfz = abs(hz - dim3); boxi = x; } } else { if (dim2 - hy < bbfy) { bboxx = dim1; bboxy = dim2; bboxz = dim3; bbfx = hmx - dim1; bbfy = dim2 - hy; bbfz = abs(hz - dim3); bboxi = x; } else if (dim2 - hy == bbfy && hmx - dim1 < bbfx) { bboxx = dim1; bboxy = dim2; bboxz = dim3; bbfx = hmx - dim1; bbfy = dim2 - hy; bbfz = abs(hz - dim3); bboxi = x; } else if (dim2 - hy == bbfy && hmx - dim1 == bbfx && abs(hz - dim3) < bbfz) { bboxx = dim1; bboxy = dim2; bboxz = dim3; bbfx = hmx - dim1; bbfy = dim2 - hy; bbfz = abs(hz - dim3); bboxi = x; } } } } void Boxologic::find_smallest_z() { scrap_min_z = scrap_list.begin(); for (auto it = scrap_list.begin(); it != scrap_list.end(); it++) if (it->cumz < scrap_min_z->cumz) scrap_min_z = it; //struct Scrappad *scrapmemb = scrap_first; //scrap_min_z = scrapmemb; //while (!(scrapmemb->next == NULL)) //{ // if (scrapmemb->next->cumz < scrap_min_z->cumz) // { // scrap_min_z = scrapmemb->next; // } // scrapmemb = scrapmemb->next; //} //return; } void Boxologic::checkfound() { evened = 0; if (boxi) { cboxi = boxi; cboxx = boxx; cboxy = boxy; cboxz = boxz; } else { auto &left = fetch_scrap_min_z_left(); auto &right = fetch_scrap_min_z_right(); if ((bboxi > 0) && (layerinlayer || (left == scrap_list.end() && right == scrap_list.end()))) { //////////////////////////////////////////// // ~ OR SCRAP_MIN_Z HAS NO NEIGHBOR //////////////////////////////////////////// if (!layerinlayer) { prelayer = layer_thickness; lilz = scrap_min_z->cumz; } cboxi = bboxi; cboxx = bboxx; cboxy = bboxy; cboxz = bboxz; layerinlayer = layerinlayer + bboxy - layer_thickness; layer_thickness = bboxy; } else { if (left == scrap_list.end() && right == scrap_list.end()) { ////// // ^~ AND SCRAP_MIN_Z HAS NO NEIGHBOR ////// layerdone = true; } else { evened = true; if (left == scrap_list.end()) { /////////////////////////////////////////// // NO LEFT, BUT RIGHT /////////////////////////////////////////// // ERASE SCRAP_MIN_Z // RIGHT IS THE NEW SCRAP_MIN_Z scrap_min_z = scrap_list.erase(scrap_min_z); //struct Scrappad *trash = scrap_min_z->next; //scrap_min_z->cumx = scrap_min_z->next->cumx; //scrap_min_z->cumz = scrap_min_z->next->cumz; //scrap_min_z->next = scrap_min_z->next->next; //if (scrap_min_z->next) //{ // scrap_min_z->next->prev = scrap_min_z; //} //free(trash); } else if (right == scrap_list.end()) { /////////////////////////////////////////// // NO RIGHT, BUT LEFT /////////////////////////////////////////// // ERASE CURRENT SCRAP_MIN_Z // THE LEFT ITEM FETCHES MIN'S CUM_X left->cumx = scrap_min_z->cumx; // ERASE FROM MIN_Z TO END //scrap_list.erase(scrap_min_z, scrap_list.end()); //scrap_min_z = scrap_list.end(); scrap_min_z = scrap_list.erase(scrap_min_z, scrap_list.end()); //scrap_min_z->prev->next = NULL; //scrap_min_z->prev->cumx = scrap_min_z->cumx; //free(scrap_min_z); } else { /////////////////////////////////////////// // LEFT & RIGHT ARE ALL EXIST /////////////////////////////////////////// if (left->cumz == right->cumz) { // ---------------------------------------- // LEFT AND RIGHT'S CUM_Z ARE EQUAL // ---------------------------------------- // LEFT FETCHES THE RIGHT'S CUM_X left->cumx = right->cumx; // ERASE MIN AND ITS RIGHT auto right_of_right = right; right_of_right++; //scrap_list.erase(scrap_min_z, right_of_right); //scrap_min_z = scrap_list.end(); scrap_min_z = scrap_list.erase(scrap_min_z, right_of_right); free(scrap_min_z);*/ } else { // ---------------------------------------- // LEFT AND RIGHT'S CUM_Z ARE NOT EQUAL // ---------------------------------------- if (left->cumz == right->cumz) left->cumx = scrap_min_z->cumx; } void Boxologic::volume_check() { box_array[cboxi].is_packed = true; box_array[cboxi].layout_width = cboxx; box_array[cboxi].layout_height = cboxy; box_array[cboxi].layout_length = cboxz; packed_volume = packed_volume + box_array[cboxi].volume; packed_boxes++; if (packing_best) { // boxologic은 따로이 최적 방향을 저장하지 않으니 // 별도의 핸들링이 필요하다 write_boxlist_file(); } else if (packed_volume == pallet.volume || packed_volume == total_box_volume) { packing = false; hundred_percent = true; } return; } void Boxologic::report_results(void) { switch (best_variant) { case 1: pallet.layout_width = pallet.width; pallet.layout_height = pallet.height; pallet.layout_length = pallet.length; break; case 2: pallet.layout_width = pallet.length; pallet.layout_height = pallet.height; pallet.layout_length = pallet.width; break; case 3: pallet.layout_width = pallet.length; pallet.layout_height = pallet.width; pallet.layout_length = pallet.height; break; case 4: pallet.layout_width = pallet.height; pallet.layout_height = pallet.width; pallet.layout_length = pallet.length; break; case 5: pallet.layout_width = pallet.width; pallet.layout_height = pallet.length; pallet.layout_length = pallet.height; break; case 6: pallet.layout_width = pallet.height; pallet.layout_height = pallet.length; pallet.layout_length = pallet.width; break; } packing_best = true; packed_box_percentage = best_solution_volume * 100 / total_box_volume; pallet_volume_used_percentage = best_solution_volume * 100 / pallet.volume; list_candidate_layers(); packed_volume = 0.0; packedy = 0; packing = true; layer_thickness = best_iteration; remainpy = pallet.layout_height; remainpz = pallet.layout_length; for (size_t x = 1; x <= total_boxes; x++) { box_array[x].is_packed = false; } do { layerinlayer = 0; layerdone = 0; pack_layer(); packedy = packedy + layer_thickness; remainpy = pallet.layout_height - packedy; if (layerinlayer) { prepackedy = packedy; preremainpy = remainpy; remainpy = layer_thickness - prelayer; packedy = packedy - layer_thickness + prelayer; remainpz = lilz; layer_thickness = layerinlayer; layerdone = 0; pack_layer(); packedy = prepackedy; remainpy = preremainpy; remainpz = pallet.layout_length; } find_layer(remainpy); } while (packing); } void Boxologic::write_boxlist_file() { double x, y, z, bx, by, bz; switch (best_variant) { case 1: x = box_array[cboxi].cox; y = box_array[cboxi].coy; z = box_array[cboxi].coz; bx = box_array[cboxi].layout_width; by = box_array[cboxi].layout_height; bz = box_array[cboxi].layout_length; break; case 2: x = box_array[cboxi].coz; y = box_array[cboxi].coy; z = box_array[cboxi].cox; bx = box_array[cboxi].layout_length; by = box_array[cboxi].layout_height; bz = box_array[cboxi].layout_width; break; case 3: x = box_array[cboxi].coy; y = box_array[cboxi].coz; z = box_array[cboxi].cox; bx = box_array[cboxi].layout_height; by = box_array[cboxi].layout_length; bz = box_array[cboxi].layout_width; break; case 4: x = box_array[cboxi].coy; y = box_array[cboxi].cox; z = box_array[cboxi].coz; bx = box_array[cboxi].layout_height; by = box_array[cboxi].layout_width; bz = box_array[cboxi].layout_length; break; case 5: x = box_array[cboxi].cox; y = box_array[cboxi].coz; z = box_array[cboxi].coy; bx = box_array[cboxi].layout_width; by = box_array[cboxi].layout_length; bz = box_array[cboxi].layout_height; break; case 6: x = box_array[cboxi].coz; y = box_array[cboxi].cox; z = box_array[cboxi].coy; bx = box_array[cboxi].layout_length; by = box_array[cboxi].layout_width; bz = box_array[cboxi].layout_height; break; } box_array[cboxi].cox = x; box_array[cboxi].coy = y; box_array[cboxi].coz = z; box_array[cboxi].layout_width = bx; box_array[cboxi].layout_height = by; box_array[cboxi].layout_length = bz; }
250  best_solution_volume = packed_volume;
251  best_variant = variant;
252  best_iteration = itelayer;
253  number_packed_boxes = packed_boxes;

273 void Boxologic::list_candidate_layers()
274 {
275  double exdim; // 기준으로 삼을 축에서의 크기 double dimdif; double dimen2, dimen3; // 기준 외 잔여 축에서의 크기 size_t x, y, z; double layereval; for (x = 1; x <= total_boxes; x++) { for (y = 1; y <= 3; y++) { // 기준 축으로부터 기준 크기 (key) 를 뽑아옴 switch (y) { case 1: exdim = box_array[x].width; dimen2 = box_array[x].height; dimen3 = box_array[x].length; break; case 2: exdim = box_array[x].height; dimen2 = box_array[x].width; dimen3 = box_array[x].length; break; case 3: exdim = box_array[x].length; dimen2 = box_array[x].width; dimen3 = box_array[x].height; break; } if ((exdim > pallet.layout_height) || (((dimen2 > pallet.layout_width) || (dimen3 > pallet.layout_length)) && ((dimen3 > pallet.layout_width) || (dimen2 > pallet.layout_length)))) { // 박스가 화물칸보다 큰 경우 continue; } // 기존 레이어와 중복되면 SKIP if (layer_map.count(exdim) != 0) continue; layereval = 0; // 모든 박스의 최소 크기 (각 박스의 x, y, z축 내 최소 크기) 를 구하여 // 현재 레이어에 쌓는다 (layereval에 더한다) for (z = 1; z <= total_boxes; z++) { if (!(x == z)) { dimdif = abs(exdim - box_array[z].width); if (abs(exdim - box_array[z].height) < dimdif) { dimdif = abs(exdim - box_array[z].height); } if (abs(exdim - box_array[z].length) < dimdif) { dimdif = abs(exdim - box_array[z].length); } layereval = layereval + dimdif; } } // 레이어 크기와 기준값을 기록함 layer_map[exdim] = layereval; } } return; } int Boxologic::pack_layer() { double lenx, lenz, lpz; if (!layer_thickness) { packing = false; return 0; } scrap_list.begin()->cumx = pallet.layout_width; scrap_list.begin()->cumz = 0; while (1) { // INIT SCRAP_MIN_Z find_smallest_z(); // FETCH LEFT AND RIGHT OF SCRAP_MIN_Z auto &left = fetch_scrap_min_z_left(); auto &right = fetch_scrap_min_z_right(); lpz = remainpz - scrap_min_z->cumz; find_box(lenx, layer_thickness, remainpy, lpz, lpz); checkfound(); if (layerdone) break; if (evened) continue; // RE-FETCH LEFT AND RIGHT left = fetch_scrap_min_z_left(); right = fetch_scrap_min_z_right(); box_array[cboxi].cox = 0; box_array[cboxi].coy = packedy; box_array[cboxi].coz = scrap_min_z->cumz; if (cboxx == scrap_min_z->cumx) { scrap_min_z->cumz = scrap_min_z->cumz + cboxz; //(scrap_min_z->prev)->cumz = scrap_min_z->cumz + cboxz; } } volume_check(); } } return 0; } int Boxologic::find_layer(double thickness) { double exdim, dimdif, dimen2, dimen3; double layereval, eval; } if (abs(exdim - box_array[z].length) < dimdif) { dimdif = abs(exdim - box_array[z].length); } layereval = layereval + dimdif; } } if (layereval < eval) { eval = layereval; layer_thickness = exdim; } } } } if (layer_thickness == 0 || layer_thickness > remainpy) packing = false; return 0; } void Boxologic::find_box(double hmx, double hy, double hmy, double hz, double hmz) { bfx = 32767; bfy = 32767; bfz = 32767; bbfx = 32767; bbfy = 32767; bbfz = 32767; boxi = 0; bboxi = 0; for (size_t x = 1; analyze_box(x, hmx, hy, hmy, hz, hmz, box_array[x].width, box_array[x].length, box_array[x].height); analyze_box(x, hmx, hy, hmy, hz, hmz, box_array[x].height, box_array[x].width, box_array[x].length); analyze_box(x, hmx, hy, hmy, hz, hmz, box_array[x].height, box_array[x].length, box_array[x].width); analyze_box(x, hmx, hy, hmy, hz, hmz, box_array[x].length, box_array[x].width, box_array[x].height); analyze_box(x, hmx, hy, hmy, hz, hmz, box_array[x].length, box_array[x].height, box_array[x].width); } } void Boxologic::analyze_box(size_t x, double hmx, double hy, double hmy, double hz, double hmz, double dim1, double dim2, double dim3) { if (dim1 <= hmx && dim2 <= hmy && dim3 <= hmz) { if (dim2 <= hy) { if (hy - dim2 < bfy) { boxx = dim1; boxy = dim2; boxz = dim3; bfx = hmx - dim1; bfy = hy - dim2; bfz = abs(hz - dim3); boxi = x; } else if (hy - dim2 == bfy && hmx - dim1 < bfx) { boxx = dim1; boxy = dim2; boxz = dim3; bfx = hmx - dim1; bfy = hy - dim2; bfz = abs(hz - dim3); boxi = x; } else if (hy - dim2 == bfy && hmx - dim1 == bfx && abs(hz - dim3) < bfz) { boxx = dim1; boxy = dim2; boxz = dim3; bfx = hmx - dim1; bfy = hy - dim2; bfz = abs(hz - dim3); boxi = x; } } else { if (dim2 - hy < bbfy) { bboxx = dim1; bboxy = dim2; bboxz = dim3; bbfx = hmx - dim1; bbfy = dim2 - hy; bbfz = abs(hz - dim3); bboxi = x; } else if (dim2 - hy == bbfy && hmx - dim1 < bbfx) { bboxx = dim1; bboxy = dim2; bboxz = dim3; bbfx = hmx - dim1; bbfy = dim2 - hy; bbfz = abs(hz - dim3); bboxi = x; } else if (dim2 - hy == bbfy && hmx - dim1 == bbfx && abs(hz - dim3) < bbfz) { bboxx = dim1; bboxy = dim2; bboxz = dim3; bbfx = hmx - dim1; bbfy = dim2 - hy; bbfz = abs(hz - dim3); bboxi = x; } } } } void Boxologic::find_smallest_z() { scrap_min_z = scrap_list.begin(); for (auto it = scrap_list.begin(); it != scrap_list.end(); // } // scrapmemb = scrapmemb->next; //} //return; } void Boxologic::checkfound() { evened = 0; if (boxi) { cboxi = boxi; cboxx = boxx; cboxy = boxy; cboxz = boxz; } else { auto &left = fetch_scrap_min_z_left(); //scrap_min_z->prev->cumx = scrap_min_z->cumx; //free(scrap_min_z); } else { /////////////////////////////////////////// // LEFT & RIGHT ARE ALL EXIST /////////////////////////////////////////// if (left->cumz == right->cumz) { // ---------------------------------------- // LEFT AND RIGHT'S CUM_Z ARE EQUAL // ---------------------------------------- // LEFT FETCHES THE RIGHT'S CUM_X left->cumx = right->cumx; } void Boxologic::volume_check() { box_array[cboxi].is_packed = true; box_array[cboxi].layout_width = cboxx; box_array[cboxi].layout_height = cboxy; box_array[cboxi].layout_length = cboxz; packed_volume = packed_volume + box_array[cboxi].volume; packed_boxes++; if (packing_best) { // boxologic은 따로이 최적 방향을 저장하지 않으니 // 별도의 핸들링이 필요하다 write_boxlist_file(); } else if (packed_volume == pallet.volume || packed_volume == total_box_volume) { packing = false; hundred_percent = true; } return; } void Boxologic::report_results(void) { switch (best_variant) { case 1: pallet.layout_width = pallet.width; pallet.layout_height = pallet.height; pallet.layout_length = pallet.length; break; case 2: pallet.layout_width = pallet.length; pallet.layout_height = pallet.height; pallet.layout_length = pallet.width; break; case 3: pallet.layout_width = pallet.length; pallet.layout_height = pallet.width; pallet.layout_length = pallet.height; break; case 4: pallet.layout_width = pallet.height; pallet.layout_height = pallet.width; pallet.layout_length = pallet.length; break; case 5: pallet.layout_width = pallet.width; pallet.layout_height = pallet.length; pallet.layout_length = pallet.height; break; case 6: pallet.layout_width = pallet.height; pallet.layout_height = pallet.length; pallet.layout_length = pallet.width; break; } packing_best = true; packed_box_percentage = best_solution_volume * 100 / total_box_volume; pallet_volume_used_percentage = best_solution_volume * 100 / pallet.volume; list_candidate_layers(); packed_volume = 0.0; packedy = 0; packing = true; layer_thickness = best_iteration; remainpy = pallet.layout_height; remainpz = pallet.layout_length; for (size_t x = 1; x <= total_boxes; x++) { box_array[x].is_packed = false; } do { layerinlayer = 0; layerdone = 0; pack_layer(); packedy = packedy + layer_thickness; remainpy = pallet.layout_height - packedy; if (layerinlayer) { prepackedy = packedy; preremainpy = remainpy; remainpy = layer_thickness - prelayer; packedy = packedy - layer_thickness + prelayer; remainpz = lilz; layer_thickness = layerinlayer; layerdone = 0; pack_layer(); packedy = prepackedy; remainpy = preremainpy; remainpz = pallet.layout_length; } find_layer(remainpy); } while (packing); } void Boxologic::write_boxlist_file() { double x, y, z, bx, by, bz; switch (best_variant) { case 1: x = box_array[cboxi].cox; y = box_array[cboxi].coy; z = box_array[cboxi].coz; bx = box_array[cboxi].layout_width; by = box_array[cboxi].layout_height; bz = box_array[cboxi].layout_length; break; case 2: x = box_array[cboxi].coz; y = box_array[cboxi].coy; z = box_array[cboxi].cox; bx = box_array[cboxi].layout_length; by = box_array[cboxi].layout_height; bz = box_array[cboxi].layout_width; break; case 3: x = box_array[cboxi].coy; } void Boxologic::volume_check() { box_array[cboxi].is_packed = true; box_array[cboxi].layout_width = cboxx; box_array[cboxi].layout_height = cboxy; box_array[cboxi].layout_length = cboxz; packed_volume = packed_volume + box_array[cboxi].volume; hundred_percent = true; } return; } void Boxologic::report_results(void) { switch (best_variant) { case 1: pallet.layout_width = pallet.width; pallet.layout_height = pallet.height; pallet.layout_length = pallet.length; break; } packing_best = true; packed_box_percentage = best_solution_volume * 100 / total_box_volume; pallet_volume_used_percentage = best_solution_volume * 100 / pallet.volume; list_candidate_layers(); //(scrap_min_z->prev)->cumz = scrap_min_z->cumz + cboxz; } } volume_check(); } } return 0; } int Boxologic::find_layer(double thickness) { double exdim, dimdif, dimen2, dimen3; double layereval, eval; return 0; } void Boxologic::find_box(double hmx, double hy, double hmy, double hz, double hmz) { bfx = 32767; bfy = 32767; bfz = 32767; bbfx = 32767; bbfy = 32767; bbfz = 32767; boxi = 0; bboxi = 0; for (size_t x = 1; analyze_box(x, hmx, hy, hmy, hz, hmz, box_array[x].length, box_array[x].height, box_array[x].width); } } void Boxologic::analyze_box(size_t x, double hmx, double hy, double hmy, double hz, double hmz, double dim1, double dim2, double dim3) { if (dim1 <= hmx && dim2 <= hmy && dim3 <= hmz) { if (dim2 <= hy) { if (hy - dim2 < bfy) { boxx = dim1; boxy = dim2; boxz = dim3; bfx = hmx - dim1; bfy = hy - dim2; bfz = abs(hz - dim3); boxi = x; } else if (hy - dim2 == bfy && hmx - dim1 < bfx) { boxx = dim1; boxy = dim2; boxz = dim3; bfx = hmx - dim1; bfy = hy - dim2; bfz = abs(hz - dim3); boxi = x; } else if (hy - dim2 == bfy && hmx - dim1 == bfx && abs(hz - dim3) < bfz) { boxx = dim1; boxy = dim2; boxz = dim3; bfx = hmx - dim1; bfy = hy - dim2; bfz = abs(hz - dim3); boxi = x; } } else { if (dim2 - hy < bbfy) { bboxx = dim1; bboxy = dim2; bboxz = dim3; bbfx = hmx - dim1; bbfy = dim2 - hy; bbfz = abs(hz - dim3); bboxi = x; } else if (dim2 - hy == bbfy && hmx - dim1 < bbfx) { bboxx = dim1; bboxy = dim2; bboxz = dim3; bbfx = hmx - dim1; bbfy = dim2 - hy; bbfz = abs(hz - dim3); bboxi = x; } else if (dim2 - hy == bbfy && hmx - dim1 == bbfx && abs(hz - dim3) < bbfz) { bboxx = dim1; bboxy = dim2; bboxz = dim3; bbfx = hmx - dim1; bbfy = dim2 - hy; bbfz = abs(hz - dim3); bboxi = x; } } } } void Boxologic::find_smallest_z() { scrap_min_z = scrap_list.begin(); for (auto it = scrap_list.begin(); it != scrap_list.end(); it++) if (it->cumz < scrap_min_z->cumz) scrap_min_z = it; //struct Scrappad *scrapmemb = scrap_first; //scrap_min_z = scrapmemb; //while (!(scrapmemb->next == NULL)) //{ // if (scrapmemb->next->cumz < scrap_min_z->cumz) // { // scrap_min_z = scrapmemb->next; // } // scrapmemb = scrapmemb->next; //} //return; } void Boxologic::checkfound() { evened = 0; if (boxi) { cboxi = boxi; cboxx = boxx; cboxy = boxy; cboxz = boxz; } else { auto &left = fetch_scrap_min_z_left(); auto &right = fetch_scrap_min_z_right(); if ((bboxi > 0) && (layerinlayer || (left == scrap_list.end() && right == scrap_list.end()))) { //////////////////////////////////////////// // ~ OR SCRAP_MIN_Z HAS NO NEIGHBOR //////////////////////////////////////////// if (!layerinlayer) { prelayer = layer_thickness; lilz = scrap_min_z->cumz; } cboxi = bboxi; cboxx = bboxx; cboxy = bboxy; cboxz = bboxz; layerinlayer = layerinlayer + bboxy - layer_thickness; layer_thickness = bboxy; } else { if (left == scrap_list.end() && right == scrap_list.end()) { ////// // ^~ AND SCRAP_MIN_Z HAS NO NEIGHBOR ////// layerdone = true; } else { evened = true; if (left == scrap_list.end()) { /////////////////////////////////////////// // NO LEFT, BUT RIGHT /////////////////////////////////////////// // ERASE SCRAP_MIN_Z // RIGHT IS THE NEW SCRAP_MIN_Z scrap_min_z = scrap_list.erase(scrap_min_z); //struct Scrappad *trash = scrap_min_z->next; //scrap_min_z->cumx = scrap_min_z->next->cumx; //scrap_min_z->cumz = scrap_min_z->next->cumz; //scrap_min_z->next = scrap_min_z->next->next; //if (scrap_min_z->next) //{ // scrap_min_z->next->prev = scrap_min_z; //} //free(trash); } else if (right == scrap_list.end()) { /////////////////////////////////////////// // NO RIGHT, BUT LEFT /////////////////////////////////////////// // ERASE CURRENT SCRAP_MIN_Z // THE LEFT ITEM FETCHES MIN'S CUM_X left->cumx = scrap_min_z->cumx; // ERASE FROM MIN_Z TO END //scrap_list.erase(scrap_min_z, scrap_list.end()); //scrap_min_z = scrap_list.end(); scrap_min_z = scrap_list.erase(scrap_min_z, scrap_list.end()); //scrap_min_z->prev->next = NULL; //scrap_min_z->prev->cumx = scrap_min_z->cumx; //free(scrap_min_z); } else { /////////////////////////////////////////// // LEFT & RIGHT ARE ALL EXIST /////////////////////////////////////////// if (left->cumz == right->cumz) { // ---------------------------------------- // LEFT AND RIGHT'S CUM_Z ARE EQUAL // ---------------------------------------- // LEFT FETCHES THE RIGHT'S CUM_X left->cumx = right->cumx; // ERASE MIN AND ITS RIGHT auto right_of_right = right; right_of_right++; //scrap_list.erase(scrap_min_z, right_of_right); //scrap_min_z = scrap_list.end(); scrap_min_z = scrap_list.erase(scrap_min_z, right_of_right); /*scrap_min_z->prev->next = scrap_min_z->next->next; if (scrap_min_z->next->next) { scrap_min_z->next->next->prev = scrap_min_z->prev; } (scrap_min_z->prev)->cumx = scrap_min_z->next->cumx; free(scrap_min_z->next); free(scrap_min_z);*/ } else { // ---------------------------------------- // LEFT AND RIGHT'S CUM_Z ARE NOT EQUAL // ---------------------------------------- if (left->cumz == right->cumz) left->cumx = scrap_min_z->cumx; //scrap_list.erase(scrap_min_z); //scrap_min_z = scrap_list.end(); scrap_min_z = scrap_list.erase(scrap_min_z); //scrap_min_z->prev->next = scrap_min_z->next; //scrap_min_z->next->prev = scrap_min_z->prev; //if (scrap_min_z->prev->cumz < scrap_min_z->next->cumz) //{ // // IF LEFT'S CUM_Z IS LESS THAN RIGHT'S OWN // scrap_min_z->prev->cumx = scrap_min_z->cumx; //} //// ERASE MIN //free(scrap_min_z); } } } } } return; } void Boxologic::volume_check() { box_array[cboxi].is_packed = true; box_array[cboxi].layout_width = cboxx; box_array[cboxi].layout_height = cboxy; box_array[cboxi].layout_length = cboxz; packed_volume = packed_volume + box_array[cboxi].volume; packed_boxes++; if (packing_best) { // boxologic은 따로이 최적 방향을 저장하지 않으니 // 별도의 핸들링이 필요하다 write_boxlist_file(); } else if (packed_volume == pallet.volume || packed_volume == total_box_volume) { packing = false; hundred_percent = true; } return; } void Boxologic::report_results(void) { switch (best_variant) { case 1: pallet.layout_width = pallet.width; pallet.layout_height = pallet.height; pallet.layout_length = pallet.length; break; case 2: pallet.layout_width = pallet.length; pallet.layout_height = pallet.height; pallet.layout_length = pallet.width; break; case 3: pallet.layout_width = pallet.length; pallet.layout_height = pallet.width; pallet.layout_length = pallet.height; break; case 4: pallet.layout_width = pallet.height; pallet.layout_height = pallet.width; pallet.layout_length = pallet.length; break; case 5: pallet.layout_width = pallet.width; pallet.layout_height = pallet.length; pallet.layout_length = pallet.height; break; case 6: pallet.layout_width = pallet.height; pallet.layout_height = pallet.length; pallet.layout_length = pallet.width; break; } packing_best = true; packed_box_percentage = best_solution_volume * 100 / total_box_volume; pallet_volume_used_percentage = best_solution_volume * 100 / pallet.volume; list_candidate_layers(); packed_volume = 0.0; packedy = 0; packing = true; layer_thickness = best_iteration; remainpy = pallet.layout_height; remainpz = pallet.layout_length; for (size_t x = 1; x <= total_boxes; x++) { box_array[x].is_packed = false; } do { layerinlayer = 0; layerdone = 0; pack_layer(); packedy = packedy + layer_thickness; remainpy = pallet.layout_height - packedy; if (layerinlayer) { prepackedy = packedy; preremainpy = remainpy; remainpy = layer_thickness - prelayer; packedy = packedy - layer_thickness + prelayer; remainpz = lilz; layer_thickness = layerinlayer; layerdone = 0; pack_layer(); packedy = prepackedy; remainpy = preremainpy; remainpz = pallet.layout_length; } find_layer(remainpy); } while (packing); } void Boxologic::write_boxlist_file() { double x, y, z, bx, by, bz; switch (best_variant) { case 1: x = box_array[cboxi].cox; y = box_array[cboxi].coy; z = box_array[cboxi].coz; bx = box_array[cboxi].layout_width; by = box_array[cboxi].layout_height; bz = box_array[cboxi].layout_length; break; case 2: x = box_array[cboxi].coz; y = box_array[cboxi].coy; z = box_array[cboxi].cox; bx = box_array[cboxi].layout_length; by = box_array[cboxi].layout_height; bz = box_array[cboxi].layout_width; break; case 3: x = box_array[cboxi].coy; y = box_array[cboxi].coz; z = box_array[cboxi].cox; bx = box_array[cboxi].layout_height; by = box_array[cboxi].layout_length; bz = box_array[cboxi].layout_width; break; case 4: x = box_array[cboxi].coy; y = box_array[cboxi].cox; z = box_array[cboxi].coz; bx = box_array[cboxi].layout_height; by = box_array[cboxi].layout_width; bz = box_array[cboxi].layout_length; break; case 5: x = box_array[cboxi].cox; y = box_array[cboxi].coz; z = box_array[cboxi].coy; bx = box_array[cboxi].layout_width; by = box_array[cboxi].layout_length; bz = box_array[cboxi].layout_height; break; case 6: x = box_array[cboxi].coz; y = box_array[cboxi].cox; z = box_array[cboxi].coy; bx = box_array[cboxi].layout_length; by = box_array[cboxi].layout_width; bz = box_array[cboxi].layout_height; break; } box_array[cboxi].cox = x; box_array[cboxi].coy = y; box_array[cboxi].coz = z; box_array[cboxi].layout_width = bx; box_array[cboxi].layout_height = by; box_array[cboxi].layout_length = bz; }
337  layer_map[exdim] = layereval;
338  }
339  }

343 int Boxologic::pack_layer()
344 {
345  double lenx, lenz, lpz;
346 
347  if (!layer_thickness)
348  {
349  packing = false;
350  return 0;
351  }
352 
353  scrap_list.begin()->cumx = pallet.layout_width;
354  scrap_list.begin()->cumz = 0;
355 
356  while (1)
357  {
358  // INIT SCRAP_MIN_Z
359  find_smallest_z();
360 
361  // FETCH LEFT AND RIGHT OF SCRAP_MIN_Z
362  auto &left = fetch_scrap_min_z_left();
363  auto &right = fetch_scrap_min_z_right();
364 
365  if (left == scrap_list.end() && right == scrap_list.end())
366  {
368  // NO LEFT AND RIGHT
370  //*** SITUATION-1: NO BOXES ON THE RIGHT AND LEFT SIDES ***
371  lenx = scrap_min_z->cumx;
372  lpz = remainpz - scrap_min_z->cumz;
373 
374  find_box(lenx, layer_thickness, remainpy, lpz, lpz);
375  checkfound();
376 
377  if (layerdone) break;
378  if (evened) continue;
379 
380  // RE-FETCH LEFT AND RIGHT
381  left = fetch_scrap_min_z_left();
382  right = fetch_scrap_min_z_right();
383 
384  box_array[cboxi].cox = 0;
385  box_array[cboxi].coy = packedy;
386  box_array[cboxi].coz = scrap_min_z->cumz;
387 
388  if (cboxx == scrap_min_z->cumx)
389  {
390  scrap_min_z->cumz = scrap_min_z->cumz + cboxz;
391  }
392  else
393  {
394  // CREATE A NEW NODE AND IT'S THE NEW MIN_Z
395  // ORDINARY MIN_Z WILL BE SHIFTED TO THE RIGHT
396  struct Scrappad node =
397  {
398  cboxx,
399  scrap_min_z->cumz + cboxz
400  };
401 
402  // SHIFTS ORDINARY MIN_Z TO RIGHT
403  // AND THE NEW NODE'S ITERATOR IS THE NEW MIN_Z FROM NOW ON
404  scrap_min_z = scrap_list.insert(scrap_min_z, node);
405 
406  /*scrap_min_z->next = (struct Scrappad*)malloc(sizeof(struct Scrappad));
407  if (scrap_min_z->next == NULL)
408  {
409  printf("Insufficient memory available\n");
410  return 1;
411  }
412  scrap_min_z->next->next = NULL;
413  scrap_min_z->next->prev = scrap_min_z;
414 
415  scrap_min_z->next->cumx = scrap_min_z->cumx;
416  scrap_min_z->next->cumz = scrap_min_z->cumz;
417 
418  scrap_min_z->cumx = cboxx;
419  scrap_min_z->cumz = scrap_min_z->cumz + cboxz;*/
420  }
421  volume_check();
422  }
423  else if (left == scrap_list.end())
424  {
425  //*** SITUATION-2: NO BOXES ON THE LEFT SIDE ***
426

429  lpz = remainpz - scrap_min_z->cumz;

432  checkfound();

439  right = fetch_scrap_min_z_right();
440

443 
444  if (cboxx == scrap_min_z->cumx)
445  {
446  box_array[cboxi].cox = 0;
447 
448  if (scrap_min_z->cumz + cboxz == right->cumz)
449  {
450  // RIGHT IS THE NEW MIN_Z
451  // ORDINARY MIN_Z WILL BE ERASED
452  scrap_min_z = scrap_list.erase(scrap_min_z);
453

466  //}

472  }
473  }

752  if (evened) continue;
753 
754  // RE-FETCH LEFT AND RIGHT
755  left = fetch_scrap_min_z_left();
756  right = fetch_scrap_min_z_right();
757 
758  box_array[cboxi].coy = packedy;
759  box_array[cboxi].coz = scrap_min_z->cumz;
760  box_array[cboxi].cox = left->cumx;
761 
762  if (cboxx == scrap_min_z->cumx - left->cumx)
763  {
764  if (scrap_min_z->cumz + cboxz == left->cumz)
765  {
766  // LEFT FETCHES MIN_Z'S
767  left->cumx = scrap_min_z->cumx;
768 
769  // ERASE MIN_Z
770  //scrap_list.erase(scrap_min_z);
771  //scrap_min_z = scrap_list.end();
772 
773  scrap_min_z = scrap_list.erase(scrap_min_z);
774 
776  //scrap_min_z->prev->cumx = scrap_min_z->cumx;
777 
779  //scrap_min_z->prev->next = scrap_min_z->next;
780  //scrap_min_z->next->prev = scrap_min_z->prev;
781  //free(scrap_min_z);
782  }
783  else
784  {
785  scrap_min_z->cumz += cboxz;
786  }
787  }
788  else
789  {
790  if (scrap_min_z->cumz + cboxz == left->cumz)
791  {
792  left->cumx += cboxx;
793  }
794  else if (scrap_min_z->cumz + cboxz == right->cumz)
795  {
796  box_array[cboxi].cox = scrap_min_z->cumx - cboxx;
797  scrap_min_z->cumx = scrap_min_z->cumx - cboxx;
798  }
799  else
800  {
801  // CREATE NODE BETWEEN LEFT AND MIN_Z
802  struct Scrappad node =
803  {
804  left->cumx + cboxx,
805  scrap_min_z->cumz + cboxz
806  };
807  scrap_list.insert(scrap_min_z, node);
808 
810  //scrap_min_z->prev->next = (struct Scrappad*)malloc(sizeof(struct Scrappad));
811  //if (scrap_min_z->prev->next == NULL)
812  //{
813  // cout << "Insufficient memory available" << endl;
814  // return 1;
815  //}
816  //(scrap_min_z->prev->next)->prev = scrap_min_z->prev;
817  //(scrap_min_z->prev->next)->next = scrap_min_z;
818  //scrap_min_z->prev = scrap_min_z->prev->next;
819 
821  //(scrap_min_z->prev)->cumx = scrap_min_z->prev->prev->cumx + cboxx;
822  //(scrap_min_z->prev)->cumz = scrap_min_z->cumz + cboxz;
823  }
824  }
825  volume_check();
826  }
827  }
828  return 0;
829 }
830 
831 int Boxologic::find_layer(double thickness)
832 {
833  double exdim, dimdif, dimen2, dimen3;
834  double layereval, eval;
835  layer_thickness = 0;
836  eval = 1000000;
837 
838  size_t y, z;
839 
840  for (size_t x = 1; x <= total_boxes; x++)
841  {
842  if (box_array[x].is_packed) continue;
843  for (y = 1; y <= 3; y++)
844  {
845  switch (y)
846  {
847  case 1:
848  exdim = box_array[x].width;
849  dimen2 = box_array[x].height;
850  dimen3 = box_array[x].length;
851  break;
852  case 2:
853  exdim = box_array[x].height;
854  dimen2 = box_array[x].width;
855  dimen3 = box_array[x].length;
856  break;
857  case 3:
858  exdim = box_array[x].length;
859  dimen2 = box_array[x].width;
860  dimen3 = box_array[x].height;
861  break;
862  }
863  layereval = 0;
864  if ((exdim <= thickness) && (((dimen2 <= pallet.layout_width) && (dimen3 <= pallet.layout_length)) || ((dimen3 <= pallet.layout_width) && (dimen2 <= pallet.layout_length))))
865  {
866  for (z = 1; z <= total_boxes; z++)
867  {
868  if (!(x == z) && !(box_array[z].is_packed))
869  {
870  dimdif = abs(exdim - box_array[z].width);
871  if (abs(exdim - box_array[z].height) < dimdif)
872  {
873  dimdif = abs(exdim - box_array[z].height);
874  }
875  if (abs(exdim - box_array[z].length) < dimdif)
876  {
877  dimdif = abs(exdim - box_array[z].length);
878  }
879  layereval = layereval + dimdif;
880  }
881  }
882  if (layereval < eval)
883  {
884  eval = layereval;
885  layer_thickness = exdim;
886  }
887  }
888  }
889  }
890  if (layer_thickness == 0 || layer_thickness > remainpy) packing = false;
891  return 0;
892 }
893 
894 void Boxologic::find_box(double hmx, double hy, double hmy, double hz, double hmz)
895 {
896  bfx = 32767; bfy = 32767; bfz = 32767;
897  bbfx = 32767; bbfy = 32767; bbfz = 32767;
898  boxi = 0; bboxi = 0;
899 
900  for (size_t x = 1; x <= total_boxes; x++)
901  {
902  if (box_array[x].is_packed)
903  continue;
904 
905  if (x > total_boxes)
906  return;
907 
908  analyze_box(x, hmx, hy, hmy, hz, hmz, box_array[x].width, box_array[x].height, box_array[x].length);
909 
910  if ((box_array[x].width == box_array[x].length) && (box_array[x].length == box_array[x].height))
911  continue;
912 
913  analyze_box(x, hmx, hy, hmy, hz, hmz, box_array[x].width, box_array[x].length, box_array[x].height);
914  analyze_box(x, hmx, hy, hmy, hz, hmz, box_array[x].height, box_array[x].width, box_array[x].length);
915  analyze_box(x, hmx, hy, hmy, hz, hmz, box_array[x].height, box_array[x].length, box_array[x].width);
916  analyze_box(x, hmx, hy, hmy, hz, hmz, box_array[x].length, box_array[x].width, box_array[x].height);
917  analyze_box(x, hmx, hy, hmy, hz, hmz, box_array[x].length, box_array[x].height, box_array[x].width);
918  }
919 }

921 void Boxologic::analyze_box(size_t x, double hmx, double hy, double hmy, double hz, double hmz, double dim1, double dim2, double dim3)
922 {
923  if (dim1 <= hmx && dim2 <= hmy && dim3 <= hmz)
924  {
925  if (dim2 <= hy)
926  {
927  if (hy - dim2 < bfy)
928  {
929  boxx = dim1;
930  boxy = dim2;
931  boxz = dim3;
932  bfx = hmx - dim1;
933  bfy = hy - dim2;
934  bfz = abs(hz - dim3);
935  boxi = x;
936  }
937  else if (hy - dim2 == bfy && hmx - dim1 < bfx)
938  {
939  boxx = dim1;
940  boxy = dim2;
941  boxz = dim3;
942  bfx = hmx - dim1;
943  bfy = hy - dim2;
944  bfz = abs(hz - dim3);
945  boxi = x;
946  }
947  else if (hy - dim2 == bfy && hmx - dim1 == bfx && abs(hz - dim3) < bfz)
948  {
949  boxx = dim1;
950  boxy = dim2;
951  boxz = dim3;
952  bfx = hmx - dim1;
953  bfy = hy - dim2;
954  bfz = abs(hz - dim3);
955  boxi = x;
956  }
957  }
958  else
959  {
960  if (dim2 - hy < bbfy)
961  {
962  bboxx = dim1;
963  bboxy = dim2;
964  bboxz = dim3;
965  bbfx = hmx - dim1;
966  bbfy = dim2 - hy;
967  bbfz = abs(hz - dim3);
968  bboxi = x;
969  }
970  else if (dim2 - hy == bbfy && hmx - dim1 < bbfx)
971  {
972  bboxx = dim1;
973  bboxy = dim2;
974  bboxz = dim3;
975  bbfx = hmx - dim1;
976  bbfy = dim2 - hy;
977  bbfz = abs(hz - dim3);
978  bboxi = x;
979  }
980  else if (dim2 - hy == bbfy && hmx - dim1 == bbfx && abs(hz - dim3) < bbfz)
981  {
982  bboxx = dim1;
983  bboxy = dim2;
984  bboxz = dim3;
985  bbfx = hmx - dim1;
986  bbfy = dim2 - hy;
987  bbfz = abs(hz - dim3);
988  bboxi = x;
989  }
990  }
991  }
992 }

1107  {

1110  // ----------------------------------------

1138  left->cumx = scrap_min_z->cumx;

1185 
1186 void Boxologic::report_results(void)
1187 {
1188  switch (best_variant)
1189  {
1190  case 1:
1191  pallet.layout_width = pallet.width; pallet.layout_height = pallet.height; pallet.layout_length = pallet.length;
1192  break;
1193  case 2:

1195  break;

1204  break;
1205  case 6:

1210 
1211  packed_box_percentage = best_solution_volume * 100 / total_box_volume;

1216  packedy = 0;
1217  packing = true;
1218 
1219  layer_thickness = best_iteration;
1220  remainpy = pallet.layout_height;
1221  remainpz = pallet.layout_length;
1222 
1223  for (size_t x = 1; x <= total_boxes; x++)

1225  box_array[x].is_packed = false;
1226  }
1227

1231  layerdone = 0;
1232  pack_layer();
1233  packedy = packedy + layer_thickness;
1234  remainpy = pallet.layout_height - packedy;
1235 
1236  if (layerinlayer)
1237  {

1239  preremainpy = remainpy;
1240  remainpy = layer_thickness - prelayer;
1241  packedy = packedy - layer_thickness + prelayer;
1242  remainpz = lilz;
1243  layer_thickness = layerinlayer;
1244  layerdone = 0;
1245  pack_layer();

1247  remainpy = preremainpy;
1248  remainpz = pallet.layout_length;
1249  }

1251  }
